### <a name="skype-for-business-online-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="6663f-2505">Skype for Business Online の制限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2505">Skype for Business Online limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="6663f-2506">Skype for Business Online の制限は、以下のカテゴリに分類されます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2506">The limits in Skype for Business Online fall into the following categories:</span></span>
  
- [<span data-ttu-id="6663f-2507">ピアツーピア制限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2507">Peer-to-peer limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#peer-to-peer-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="6663f-2508">会議の制限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2508">Meeting limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#meeting-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="6663f-2509">会議の保存期限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2509">Meeting retention limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#meeting-retention-limits)
    
- [<span data-ttu-id="6663f-2510">分数の制限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2510">Minute limits</span></span>](../skype-for-business-online-service-description/skype-for-business-online-limits.md#minute-limits)
    
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="6663f-2511">Microsoft 365 組織に適用される制限は、その組織がサービスに登録されている期間によって異なる場合があります。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2511">The limits applied to a Microsoft 365 organization can differ depending on how long the organization has been enrolled in the service.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="6663f-2512">Microsoft データセンターで制限が変更されると、既存のすべてのユーザーにその変更が適用されるまでしばらく時間がかかる可能性があります。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2512">When a limit is changed in the Microsoft data centers, it can take some time to apply the change to all existing customers.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="peer-to-peer-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="6663f-2513">ピアツーピア制限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2513">Peer-to-peer limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6663f-p209">**ファイル転送制限**Skype for Business Online IM 会話で転送できるファイルの最大サイズ。ファイル転送でブロックされるファイルの種類については、Microsoft サポートの記事「[Skype for Business Online でファイルや添付ファイルを送受信できない](https://docs.microsoft.com/SkypeForBusiness/troubleshoot/online-attachments/cant-send-receive-files-attachments)」を参照してください。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-p209">**File transfer limit** The maximum size of a file that can be transferred in a Skype for Business Online IM conversation. To learn which file types are blocked for file transfer, see the Microsoft Support article about [sending and receiving files or attachments in Skype for Business Online](https://docs.microsoft.com/SkypeForBusiness/troubleshoot/online-attachments/cant-send-receive-files-attachments).</span></span>
    
- <span data-ttu-id="6663f-2516">**開かれたタブ付き会話数の制限** Skype for Business ユーザーが同時に開くことのできる会話タブの最大数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2516">**Open tabbed conversations limit** The maximum number of conversation tabs that a Skype for Business user can have open at one time.</span></span>

#### <a name="meeting-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="6663f-2529">会議の制限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2529">Meeting limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6663f-2530">**ファイルのアップロード制限** 配布資料や PowerPoint プレゼンテーションなど、Skype for Business 会議にアップロードできるファイルの最大サイズ。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2530">**File upload limit** The maximum size of files that can be uploaded to a Skype for Business meeting, including handouts and PowerPoint presentations.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="6663f-2531">**Skype for Business 会議の参加者数** 単一の Skype for Business 会議に参加できる参加者 (プレゼンターを含む) の最大数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2531">**Participants in a Skype for Business meeting** The maximum number of participants (including the presenter) who can join a single Skype for Business meeting.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="6663f-2532">**Skype for Business 会議のプレゼンター数** 単一の Skype for Business 会議でのプレゼンターの最大数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2532">**Presenters in a Skype for Business meeting** The maximum number of presenters in a single Skype for Business meeting.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="6663f-2533">**Skype for Business Web アプリ会議の参加者数** 会議に参加できる Skype for Business Web アプリ会議参加者の最大数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2533">**Skype for Business web app meeting participants** The maximum number of Skype for Business web app meeting participants who can join a meeting.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="6663f-2534">**Skype for Business Web アプリの匿名参加者数** 会議に匿名で参加できる Skype for Business Web アプリ会議参加者の最大数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2534">**Skype for Business web app anonymous participants** The maximum number of Skype for Business web app meeting participants who can anonymously join a meeting.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="6663f-2535">**電話で参加するゲスト数** 会議に電話で参加できるゲストの最大数。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2535">**Guests joining by phone** The maximum number of guests who can call in to a meeting.</span></span>

> [!NOTE]

The full participant list remains visible to the presenters in the meeting. Also, Gallery View and IM errors are hidden from the attendees.</span></span> 
  
#### <a name="meeting-retention-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="6663f-2571">会議の保存期限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2571">Meeting retention limits</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="6663f-2572">**会議コンテンツの保存期限** 最後のユーザーが会議を退席してから、アップロードされた会議コンテンツが完全に削除されるまで Skype for Business に保持される時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2572">**Meeting content retention period** The amount of time after the last person leaves a meeting that any uploaded meeting content is retained in Skype for Business before it is permanently deleted.</span></span> 
    
- <span data-ttu-id="6663f-2573">**会議の有効期限** 会議が終了した後でユーザーが会議にアクセスできる時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2573">**Meeting expiration period** The amount of time after a meeting has ended that users can access the meeting.</span></span> 
    
> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="6663f-2574">各ユーザーは、いつでも最大 1,000 件の会議をデータベースに保存できます。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2574">Each person can have a maximum of 1000 conferences in the database at any time.</span></span>

#### <a name="minute-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="6663f-2603">分数の制限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="6663f-2603">Minute limits</span></span>
